# [Shakespeare's Weird Tales](https://huggingface.co/spaces/garima-mahato/ShakespearesWeirdTales)

This app spins weird tales from the context that you give in Shakespearen style.

![](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/garima-mahato/ERA_V3/refs/heads/main/Session12/assets/eg1.JPG)

This app is made using a decoder-like model > 124 million parameters and trained for 96 epochs with < 0.099 loss.

| Topic | Details |
|---|---|
| Number of model parameters | 137,710,080 |
| Token Size | 512 |
| Batch size | 4 |
| Number of epochs trained | 96 |
| Training Loss | 0.0635 |
| Model Code | [Code Link](https://github.com/garima-mahato/ERA_V3/blob/main/Session12/gpt_model.py) |
| Training Script | [Training File](https://github.com/garima-mahato/ERA_V3/blob/main/Session12/Session12.ipynb) |

epochs = 60
total_batches_per_epoch = 165
for i in range(9900,9900+total_batches_per_epoch*epochs):
    t0 = time.time()
    x, y = train_loader.next_batch()
    x, y = x.to(device), y.to(device)
    optimizer.zero_grad()
    # NEW CODE ADDED HERE
    with torch.autocast(device_type=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16):
        logits, loss = model(x, y)
    loss.backward()
    optimizer.step()
    # torch.cuda.synchronize()
    t1 = time.time()
    dt = (t1 - t0) * 1000
    tokens_per_sec = (train_loader.B * train_loader.T) / (t1 - t0)
    print(f'Epoch{(i//total_batches_per_epoch)+1} | step{i} | loss: {loss.item()} | dt: {dt:.2f}ms | tok/sec: {tokens_per_sec: .2f}')

    if i%(total_batches_per_epoch) == 0:
      torch.save({
            'epoch': i/total_batches_per_epoch,
            'model_state_dict': model.state_dict(),
            'optimizer_state_dict': optimizer.state_dict(),
            'loss': loss,
            }, f'drive/MyDrive/E4P2/ShakespeareModel.pt')
